# <a name="archived-release-notes-for-monthly-channel"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-103">有关每月频道的已存档发行说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-103">Archived Release notes for Monthly Channel</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-104">我们为 Office 365 专业增强版、Visio Pro for Office 365、Project Online 桌面客户端和 Office 365 商业版提供了每月频道更新。这些发行说明提供了有关这些更新中所含新功能和非安全更新的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-104">These release notes provide information about new features and non-security updates that are included in Monthly Channel updates to Office 365 ProPlus, Visio Pro for Office 365, Project Online Desktop Client and Office 365 Business.</span></span>

 > [!NOTE]
>- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-105">我们经常会过一段时间就将功能（有时甚至是修补程序）发布到每月频道更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-105">We often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Monthly over a period of time.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-106">如果没有立即看到下述内容，则很快就会看到的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-106">If you don’t see something described below right away, you can expect it soon.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-107">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-107">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/when-do-i-get-the-newest-features-in-for-office-365-da36192c-58b9-4bc9-8d51-bb6eed468516)
>- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-108">Office 365 专业增强版现有安装的 Microsoft Teams - 从 7 月初开始，Office 365 专业增强版（和 Office 365 商业版）的更新将包含 Microsoft Teams。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-108">Microsoft Teams on existing installations of Office 365 ProPlus - Beginning in early July, updates to Office 365 ProPlus (and Office 365 Business) will include Microsoft Teams.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-109">将添加 Teams 的日期取决于所使用的更新频道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-109">The date when Teams will be added depends on which update channel you're using.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-110">有关详细信息, 请参阅[使用 Office 365 专业增强版部署 Microsoft Teams](/deployoffice/teams-install)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-110">Please refer to [Deploy Microsoft Teams with Office 365 ProPlus](/deployoffice/teams-install) for additional information.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-115">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-115">Resolved issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-117">此更改通过利用软件呈现避免了某些 Intel 图形驱动程序的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-117">This change circumvents a problem with certain Intel graphics drivers by leveraging software rendering.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-118">我们修复了数据透视图的右键单击菜单，以便启用“显示详细信息”选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-118">We fixed the right click menu for Pivot Charts to enable the option to Show Details.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-120">解决了导致 Web 加载项访问数字权限管理邮件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-120">Addresses an issue that caused web add ins to access Digital Rights Managed messages.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-125">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-125">Feature updates</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-126">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-126">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-127">**键入可返回多个值的公式：** 现可键入返回多个值的公式，它们将自动溢出到相邻的单元格中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-127">**Type a formula that returns multiple values:** Quickly type a formula that returns multiple values, and they'll automatically spill into the neighboring cells.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-128">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-128">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/5c2c9cbb-def8-409a-b380-2fbf91b20aa3)

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-129">**6 个强大的函数：** 我们添加了六个新函数来增强你的电子表格：FILTER、SORT、SORTBY、UNIQUE、SEQUENCE 和 RANDARRAY。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-129">**Six powerful functions:** We’ve added six new functions to supercharge your spreadsheets: FILTER, SORT, SORTBY, UNIQUE, SEQUENCE and RANDARRAY.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-130">了解详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-130">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/003df6c7-1dcb-4388-8e2e-0fe77a0887bc)

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-131">**数据可视化工具加载项：** 从 Excel 中快速创建 Visio 流程图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-131">**Data visualizer add-in:** Quickly create Visio flowcharts from Excel.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-132">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-132">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/bee3b5aa-aaaf-4401-acc6-276b711c763c)

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-133">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-133">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-134">**共同创作改进：** 通过让其他人以更接近实时的方式接收内容更改，改进了共同创作体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-134">**Coauthoring improvements:** Improved the coauthoring experience by making it more likely that content changes will be received by others in real time.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-137">已解决的问题</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-137">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-138">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-138">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-139">解决了 Microsoft Access 中的一个问题，该问题可能会导致在运行更新查询或在 SQL 中使用 UPDATE 语句时出现&quot;查询已损坏&quot;错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-139">Fixed an issue in Microsoft Access that may cause the error &quot;Query is Corrupt&quot; when an Update Query is run, or an UPDATE statement is used in SQL.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-140">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-140">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-141">Excel 可能会在编辑不受信任的网络共享中的受保护文件时遇到问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-141">Excel may have issues when editing a protected file from an untrusted network share.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-142">解决了在无工作簿打开的情况下搜索最近使用的文件时可能导致出现崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-142">Resolved an issue that may have caused a crash when searching for recent files while no workbook is open.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-143">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-143">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-144">解决了导致用户在尝试从“帐户创建”上下文联系支持人员时看到带有“&quot;确定&quot;”按钮的空白消息框的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-144">Addressed an issue that caused users to see an empty message box with an &quot;OK&quot; button when trying to contact support from the Account Creation context.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-145">如果在 2019 年使用巴西利亚时区，则定期会议和约会将显示在 2020 年的错误时间段内。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-145">When using the Brazilia time zone in the year 2019, recurring meetings and appointments are displayed in the wrong timeslot for the year 2020.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-146">此更改涉及到在巴西利亚时区设置的客户端以及在该时区设置的会议和约会。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-146">This change is relevant for clients set in the Brazilia time zone or for meetings and appointments set in that time zone.</span></span> 

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-147">解决了导致用户在打开“规则”对话框时看到&quot;此计算机上的规则与 Microsoft Exchange 上的规则不匹配&quot;提示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-147">Addressed an issue that caused users to see a &quot;The rules on this computer do not match the rules on Microsoft Exchange&quot; prompt when opening the Rules dialog.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-148">解决了 SMIME 算法选择方面的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-148">Corrected an issue with SMIME algorithm selection.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-149">解决了导致会议中的“位置”字段意外更新的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-149">Addressed an issue that caused the Location field in meetings to get updated unexpectedly.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-150">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-150">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-151">解决了 Office 更新可能已意外地从 Office CDN 而不是计划源（例如本地/网络共享或 Configuration Manager 提供的位置）下载文件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-151">Resolved an issue where Office updates may have unexpectedly downloaded files from the Office CDN instead of the intended source, such as a local or network share, or Configuration Manager-provided location.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-152">解决了 ODT 和 GPO 更新截止时间设置中相对截止日期仅在第一次设置时起作用，而修复程序为后续更新启用相对截止日期的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-152">Fixed an issue in ODT and GPO Update Deadline setting where relative deadline only works the first time it is set, the fix enables the relative deadline for subsequent updates.</span></span>

### <a name="feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-179">功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-179">Feature updates</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-180">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-180">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-181">**创建更易于访问的 PDF：** 创建一个 PDF，辅助功能检查器将会在你进行保存前指出要修复的辅助功能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-181">**Create more accessible PDFs:** Create a PDF and the accessibility checker will point out accessibility issues to fix before you save.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-182">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-182">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/064625e0-56ea-4e16-ad71-3aa33bb4b7ed)

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-183">**将文件转换为改进辅助功能：** 将文件升级到新式格式，使其更易于所有人访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-183">**Convert files to improve accessibility:** Upgrade your files to the modern format to make them more accessible for everyone.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-184">**向文档和电子邮件应用敏感度标签：** 向文档和邮件应用敏感度标签，使其符合组织的信息保护策略。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-184">**Apply sensitivity labels to your documents and emails:** Apply sensitivity labels to your files and emails to keep them compliant with your organization's information protection policies.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-185">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-185">Learn more</span></span>](https://aka.ms/officemipdocs)

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-189">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-189">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-190">**创建更易于访问的 PDF：** 创建一个 PDF，辅助功能检查器将会在你进行保存前指出要修复的辅助功能问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-190">**Create more accessible PDFs:** Create a PDF and the accessibility checker will point out accessibility issues to fix before you save.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-191">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-191">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/064625e0-56ea-4e16-ad71-3aa33bb4b7ed)

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-192">**将文件转换为改进辅助功能：** 将文件升级到新式格式，使其更易于所有人访问。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-192">**Convert files to improve accessibility:** Upgrade your files to the modern format to make them more accessible for everyone.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-250">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-250">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-251">**Outlook 中的插入链接菜单将插入包含租户管理员定义的权限的链接：** Outlook 插入链接 MRU 中的链接将插入仅对已经拥有权限的用户有效的链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-251">**Insert Link Menu in Outlook will insert a link with permission defined by tenant admin:** A link from the Insert Link MRU in Outlook would insert a link that only worked for users who already had permissions to it.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-252">这通常会导致请求获得文档访问权限的用户之间发生往来电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-252">This often caused back and forth emails between users asking to be granted access to a document.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-253">我们已更新了此体验，现在该链接将通过租户管理员设置的默认权限进行插入。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-253">We've updated this experience so now the link is inserted with the default permission set by the tenant admin.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-254">**Outlook 可视化刷新：** 这是 Outlook 核心体验的可视化刷新的一部分，它更新了邮件在阅读窗格和检查器中的布局方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-254">**Outlook visual refresh:** This is part of the visual refresh of core experiences in Outlook, updating how mail messages layout in the reading pane and inspector.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-255">**共享日历更新速度更快：** 对于 Office 365 中的共享日历，Outlook 可以使用 REST API 更新这些日历。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-255">**Shared calendar updates just got faster:** For shared calendars in Office 365, Outlook can update these calendars using the REST API.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-256">打开预览，更快速、更可靠地更新共享日历。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-256">Turn on the preview for faster and more reliable updates to shared calendars.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-257">**查看搜索结果中的相关消息：** Outlook 会分析搜索词，并在搜索结果顶部显示最相关的电子邮件信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-257">**See relevant messages in your search results:** Outlook analyzes search terms and shows the most relevant email messages at the top of your search results.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-258">还会在“热门搜索结果”部分看到按日期排序的所有搜索结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-258">You'll also see all results sorted by date in the Top Results section.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-259">**向合适的人员发送电子邮件：** 只需单击“收件人:”行，然后从建议的联系人中进行选择。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-259">**Send the mail to the right person:** Just click the To: line and choose from suggested contacts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-260">图片和状态指示器可帮助你选择合适的人员。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-260">A picture and presence indicator helps you choose the right person.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-261">**针对攻击的高级防护：** 通过 Office 365 高级威胁防护，可通过电子邮件主题中的超链接、附加邮件、签名邮件、网络路径等方式抵御攻击。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-261">**Advanced protection against attack:** With Office 365 Advanced Threat Protection, you're protected against attacks through hyperlinks within email subjects, attached messages, signed messages, network paths, and so on.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-262">**以不同的亮度查看邮件：** 使用“太阳”/“月亮”按钮在阅读窗格中的明暗背景之间切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-262">**See your messages in a different light:** Use the Sun/Moon button to switch between light and dark backgrounds in the reading pane.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-263">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-263">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/3e2446e0-9a7b-4189-9af9-57fb94d02ae3)

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-357">**在类似列上连接表：** 在比较列时，获取和转换 (Power Query) 现在具有近似文本匹配逻辑（也称为模糊匹配），用于合并表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-357">**Join tables on similar columns:** Get & Transform (Power Query) now features approximate text matching logic (also called fuzzy matching) when comparing columns for merging tables.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="aed7d-358">了解更多</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-358">Learn more</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/ffdd5082-c0c8-4c8e-a794-bd3962b90649)

### <a name="outlook-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-705">Outlook：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-705">Outlook: Feature updates</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-p213">**缩放和粘贴：** 选择默认设置用于所有邮件，而无需在每次阅读邮件时调整缩放。[了解详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/56c090bc-e148-44a7-bd06-1290edd38983)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-p213">**Zoom and stick:** Instead of adjusting Zoom each time you read a message, choose a default to use for all your messages.  [Learn more](https://support.office.com/article/56c090bc-e148-44a7-bd06-1290edd38983)</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-708">**移动邮件时继续工作：** Outlook 现在在后台移动邮件，因此你可以在文件夹之间移动大量邮件时继续工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-708">**Keep working while moving messages:** Outlook now moves messages in the background, so you can keep working while moving lots of messages between folders.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-p214">**优化了重点收件箱的启用和禁用体验：** 对于不使用重点收件箱的客户，我们跨所有文件夹恢复了邮件列表中的“未读”选项卡。此外，我们还添加了按标志排序功能，以简化已标志项的查找过程。最后，重点收件箱改进了搜索交互模型：重点收件箱一直保留到用户开始搜索，我们在搜索完成后显示“结果”文本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-p214">**Polished the Focused Inbox on and off experiences:** For customers that do not use Focused Inbox, we brought back the Unread tab in the message list across all folders. We also added a sort by Flag to make it easier to find flagged items. Finally, Focused Inbox has a better interaction model with search: Focused Inbox remains until a user starts to search and we show 'Results' text shown after a search completes.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1161">**将 SVG 图标转换为形状：** 将所有 SVG 图片和图标都转换为 Office 形状，这样就可以更改它们的颜色、尺寸或纹理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1161">**Convert SVG icons to shapes:** Transform all SVG pictures and icons into Office shapes so you can change their color, size, or texture.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1162">**Office 365 群组的改进：** 阅读和回复群组对话比以往更加简便，因为你可以双击群组消息在其自己的窗口中打开。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1162">**Improvements to Office 365 groups:** It’s easier than ever to read and reply to group conversations because you can double-click on a group message to open it in its own window.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1163">PowerPoint：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1163">PowerPoint: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1164">**3D 动画：** 通过添加轻轻摇摆、跳跃和旋转等动画效果，让你的 3D 模型活起来。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1164">**3D animations:** Bring your 3D models to life with animations such as swinging gently or jumping and turning.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1165">**将 SVG 图标转换为形状：** 将所有 SVG 图片和图标都转换为 Office 形状，以便可更改其颜色、大小或纹理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1165">**Convert SVG icons to shapes:** Transform all SVG pictures and icons into Office shapes so you can change their color, size, or texture.</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1166">Skype for Business：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1166">Skype for Business: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1167">在用于传入 PSTN 呼叫的 Toast UI 中添加呼叫转移按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1167">Add call transfer button in the toast UI for incoming PSTN calls.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1168">当 ChatDefaultClient 和 CallDefaultClient 设置为“团队”时，通知用户呼叫和聊天正在发送到“团队”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1168">Notify users that calls and chat are being sent to Teams when ChatDefaultClient and CallDefaultClient are set to Teams.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1169">当用户不在会议中时，显示用户为“脱机”状态，并禁用 Skype for Business，同时会议加入体验设置为“本地有限客户端”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1169">Show user’s presence as Offline when user is not in a meeting and disabled from Skype for Business and meeting join experience is set to Native Limited Client.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1171">当启用与 Aries 手机和 RedirectClient 配对时，禁止新的呼叫和对话。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1171">Suppress new calls and conversations when paired with Aries phones and RedirectClient is enabled.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="aed7d-1172">修复了日期格式不是美国格式 (mm/dd/yy) 时，按日期在 PChat 中搜索消息失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="aed7d-1172">Fix an issue where searching messages in PChat by date fails when the date format is other than US format (mm/dd/yy).</span></span>
